       <img alt="51 Creative DIY Gift Wrap Ideas For Any Occasion" class="image xxxlarge " data-nid="36042893" height="1024" src="http://media2.popsugar-assets.com/files/2014/11/05/859/n/1922441/8718420990cef991_thumb_temp_cover_file157149521415032172.xxxlarge/i/DIY-Gift-Wrap.jpg" title="51 Creative DIY Gift Wrap Ideas For Any Occasion" width="1024"/>
       <figcaption class="highlightable">
        <p>
         When it comes to the holidays, there's one area we are hesitant to splurge on, and that's gift wrap. Oftentimes we use up an entire roll for a few presents, and they usually don't have the
         <a class="sugar-inline-link" href="http://www.popsugar.com/Martha-Stewart" target="_blank" title="Latest photos and news for Martha Stewart">
          Martha Stewart
         </a>
         touch. Luckily, there are tons of inexpensive
         <a class="sugar-inline-link" href="http://www.popsugar.com/DIY" target="_blank" title="Latest photos and news for DIY">
          DIY
         </a>
         gift wrap options that still look presentable and pretty. We searched the web to find the best ones you can re-create this season.
         <a href=" http://www.popsugar.com/smart-living/How-Wrap-Present-32981383">
          Newbies
         </a>
         and expert gift wrappers will love the selections below. And if you want even more, these
         <a href=" http://www.popsugar.com/smart-living/Eco-Friendly-Gift-Wrap-Ideas-32638276">
          eco-friendly
         </a>
         wrapping ideas are perfect for the environmentally conscious.
        </p>
        <p>

          </a>

         <a href="http://www.linesacross.com/2012/12/interactive-gift-wrap-for-kids.html" onclick="trackOutboundLink('article:page', 'www.linesacross.com', '36043057', 'http://www.linesacross.com/2012/12/interactive-gift-wrap-for-kids.html')" target="_blank">
